Jefferies has returned to shareholders $4.8 billion since January 2018, or 48% of shareholders' equity and 63% of tangible shareholders' equity</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">8</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> at the beginning of this effort</font></div><div style="padding-left:10.8pt;text-indent:-10.8pt"><font style="color:#b3b3b3;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%;padding-left:6.95pt">Our Board of Directors has increased our share buyback authorization back to a total of $250 million</font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#34;Our third quarter results reflect the strength and momentum of our Firm, our team, our brand and our market position, despite the challenges of the current market environment.  Investment Banking and Equities were very resilient, and we expect we have gained market share in those areas as we continue to support our clients through this volatile time.  Moreover, we achieved solid Investment Banking and Capital Markets and Asset Management net revenues of over $1.12 billion despite unrealized markdowns in our mortgage inventory and leveraged finance commitments as the current environment has particularly impacted those asset classes.  Our 14.0% adjusted annualized return on adjusted tangible equity</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">3</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> is respectable and was achieved despite the significant dislocation in the new issue capital markets for much of this period.  </font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#34;We are working very closely with our clients, so that we are able to support them further when economic and market conditions improve, and new issue activity opens up. Our backlog</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">9</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> is consistent with last quarter's levels, but realization remains dependent on market conditions. </font><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> </font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#34;2022 is feeling like a transitional year in our business, but one in which we are making good progress in enhancing our market share.  We continue to invest toward further growth, most notably in Investment Banking, guard our balance sheet and capital against the risk of the increased volatility, and prioritize our clients and our Jefferies' team.  We believe this will yield a solid result for 2022, and set the stage for continued growth and success in 2023 and beyond.&#34;</font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font><br></font></div><div Previously reported results are presented on a comparable basis.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(2)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">In the first quarter of 2022, we also made a change to present our share of the net earnings of Berkadia Commercial Mortgage Holding LLC within Investment banking net revenues, which was previously presented within our Other business category. Previously reported results are presented on a comparable basis.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(3)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Allocated net interest is not separately disaggregated for Investment Banking and Capital Markets. This presentation is aligned to our Investment Banking and Capital Markets internal performance measurement.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(4)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Includes management and performance fees from funds and accounts managed by us as well as our share of fees received by affiliated asset management companies with which we have revenue and profit share arrangements, as well as earnings on our ownership interest in affiliated asset managers.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(5)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Allocated net interest represents an allocation to Asset Management of certain of our long-term debt interest expense, net of interest income on our Cash and cash equivalents and other sources of liquidity. Allocated net interest has been disaggregated to increase transparency and to make clearer actual Investment return. We believe that aggregating Investment return and Allocated net interest would obscure the Investment return by including an amount that is unique to our credit spreads, debt maturity profile, capital structure, liquidity risks and allocation methods.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(6)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Number of trading loss days is calculated based on trading activities in our Investment Banking and Capital Markets and Asset Management business segments.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(7)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">VaR estimates the potential loss in value of trading positions in our Investment Banking and Capital Markets and Asset Management business segments due to adverse market movements over a one-day time horizon with a 95% confidence level. For a further discussion of the calculation of VaR, see &#34;Value-at-Risk&#34; in Part II, Item 7A &#34;Quantitative and Qualitative Disclosures About Market Risk&#34; in our Annual Report on Form 10-K for the year ended November 30, 2021.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt"><font><br></font></div><div and identifiable intangible assets. We believe that tangible equity is meaningful for valuation purposes, as financial companies are often measured as a multiple of tangible equity, making these ratios meaningful for investors.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(4)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Leverage ratio equals total assets divided by total equity.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(5)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Tangible gross leverage ratio (a non-GAAP financial measure) equals total assets less goodwill and identifiable intangible assets divided by tangible equity.
